<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:this.html>This</a> etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:missing.html>missing</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:incomplete.html>incomplete</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:please.html>Please</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:add.html>add</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:it.html>it</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:discuss.html>discuss</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:it.html>it</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:at.html>at</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> Etymology scriptorium.)</span>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kom.html>kom</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kommen.html>kommen</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kommetje.html>kommetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***kompres.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kompres.html>kompres</a> (43556)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">compresse</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">compressa</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kompres.html>kompres</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kompressen.html>kompressen</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kompres.html>kompresje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:compress.html>compress</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:multiply.html>multiply</a> folded <a href = vnd.unilang:cloth.html>cloth</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:apply.html>apply</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:patient.html>patient</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:s.html>s</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:skin.html>skin</a></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:kompres.html>Kompres</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">compressus</i>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kompres.html>kompres</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kompres.html>kompresser</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kompres.html>kompres</a></b> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a></i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">komprest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>compressed, condensed</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

***kool.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kool.html>kool</a> (8234)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:col.html>col</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:cole.html>cole</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kōl</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kōla</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">caulis</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
